***pluim.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pluim.html>pluim</a> (33907)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">plume</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">plūma</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">feather, down</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pluim.html>pluim</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pluimen.html>pluimen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pluim.html>pluimpje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A plume, feather</li>
<li>(<i>with indefinite article, often the diminutive: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pluim.html>pluim</a>(pje)</b></i>) A <a href = vnd.unilang:compliment.html>compliment</a>, praise, a feather on one's cap</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A plume-shaped object or part of another organ, e.g. on a butterfly's wings</li>
<li>(<i>rather the diminutive plural: <b>pluimpjes</b></i>) down</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">plume</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veer.html>veer</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">veder</span></li></ul>

***pluimage.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pluimage.html>pluimage</a> (89279)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">plumage</i>, from plume 'feather', from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pluma</i> "feather, down", from the Proto-Indo-European base *pleus- "to pluck, a feather, fleece"
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pluimage.html>pluimage</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pluimage.html>pluimages</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pluimage.html>pluimagetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>The plumage of a bird</li>
<li>(<a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a>) An object made of <a href = vnd.unilang:feathers.html>feathers</a>, mostly ornamental; also a <a href = vnd.unilang:duster.html>duster</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One's nature, typological category; notably in the expression <i><a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> divers <a href = vnd.unilang:pluimage.html>pluimage</a></i> ('of varied <a href = vnd.unilang:types.html>types</a>')</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The waving crest of a tree or wood</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">gevederte</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (a bird's <a href = vnd.unilang:feathers.html>feathers</a>)</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">pluimenbos</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">vederbos</span> (bunch of <a href = vnd.unilang:feathers.html>feathers</a>)</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">plumau</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<a href = vnd.unilang:duster.html>duster</a>)</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">pluimagebereider</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">pluimagemaker</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">lichtpluimage</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">boompluimage</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pluim.html>pluim</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:pluimage.html>pluimage</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>  <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pluumstriker</i>. </p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a sycophant, a fawner.

<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:merkt.html>Merkt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lezer.html>lezer</a> ! <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> groote <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pluimstrijker.html>pluimstrijker</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a>?

***pluspunt.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pluspunt.html>pluspunt</a> (31644)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pluspunt.html>pluspunt</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pluspunt.html>pluspunten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pluspunt.html>pluspuntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>Advantage, upside, positive characteristic.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The word <a class="mw-selflink selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:pluspunt.html>pluspunt</a></a> and its antonym <a href = vnd.unilang:minpunt.html>minpunt</a> have almost the same meaning as <a href = vnd.unilang:voordeel.html>voordeel</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:nadeel.html>nadeel</a>, but are not used in exactly the same situations. They only apply when talking about a characteristic or aspect of something. In the sentence "<a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ondervind.html>ondervind</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voordeel.html>voordeel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a>" one cannot replace <a href = vnd.unilang:voordeel.html>voordeel</a> by <a href = vnd.unilang:pluspunt.html>pluspunt</a>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:pluspunt.html>pluspunt</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> aspect <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voordeel.html>voordeel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gezien.html>gezien</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a>

***poedel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:poedel.html>poedel</a> (15132)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Pudel</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">poodle</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poedel.html>poedel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poedels.html>poedels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poedel.html>poedeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">poodle</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">dog breed</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:poedels.html>Poedels</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oorsprong.html>oorsprong</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jachthonden.html>jachthonden</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Poodles</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> originally used as hunting dogs.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">labradoedel</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poedelnaakt.html>poedelnaakt</a></span> (literally, 'naked as a poodle', starkers, from the fashion of shaving most of a poodle's fur)</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poedel.html>poedel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poedels.html>poedels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poedel.html>poedeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly ball games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A miss; a throw or shot that <a href = vnd.unilang:misses.html>misses</a> the goal or target.</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:poeder.html>poeder</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">poudre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pulvis</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">pulver</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">powder</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">poer</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gunpowder</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***poeha.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:poeha.html>poeha</a> (44840)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Uncertain: could be from the interjections <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boe.html>boe</a></span> and <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ha.html>ha</a></span>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poeha.html>poeha</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">clamor</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">fuss</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:poel.html>poel</a> (16051)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:poel.html>poel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*puol</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*pōlaz</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">poupe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">poop, stern</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">puppis</i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a vessel's stern</li>

<p>Probably an onomatopoeia (compare to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pop</i>, for senses 2, 3 and 4, or childish <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">poop</i> for sense 1).

***poespas.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:poespas.html>poespas</a> (44838)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ablauting reduplication of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poes.html>poes</a></i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> thought to have <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> an original meaning of “muck”. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Puspas</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pishpash</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mishmash</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poespas.html>poespas</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poespas.html>poespassen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poespas.html>poespasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">fuss</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">ado</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">hubbub</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mash, stew <span class="defdate">[17th <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> 19th c.]</span></li></ol>

<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>alle</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:poespas.html>poespas</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> ...</i> — all the fuss about ...</dd></dl>

***pogrom.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pogrom.html>pogrom</a> (125327)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">פּאָגראָם</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:pogrom.html>pogrom</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">погро́м</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pogróm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pogrom.html>pogrom</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pogroms.html>pogroms</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A riot aimed at persecution or massacre of a particular ethnic or religious group, usually Jews.</li>
<li>An antisemitic hate crime with a large death toll, irrespective of the number of perpetrators.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2019</b> July 17,  <a href = vnd.unilang:talia.html>Talia</a> Lavin,  “When Non-Jews Wield Anti-Semitism as Political Shield”, in  <cite>GQ</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.gq.com/story/anti-semitism-political-shield">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">More strikingly, when blood <a href = vnd.unilang:ran.html>ran</a> on the streets of Pittsburgh after the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pogrom.html>pogrom</a></b> at the Tree of Life Synagogue in 2018, Trump <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> not meet with community leaders of the Pittsburgh Jewish community, nor the family members of the dead, nor <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> the city’s mayor. He <a href = vnd.unilang:spoken.html>spoke</a> with Ron Dermer, Israel’s ambassador to the United States.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pogrom.html>pogrom</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pogroms.html>pogroms</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">pogroming</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">pogromed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To persecute or massacre a particular group of people.</li></ol>
<hr />

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">poc</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pocke</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*pukkaz</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*pukkǭ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pock; swelling</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bew-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰew-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to grow; swell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
